function set_scheme(npc, ini, scheme, section, gulag_name)
  local st = xr_logic.assign_storage_and_bind(npc, ini, scheme, section)

  st.logic     = xr_logic.cfg_get_switch_conditions(ini, section, npc)
  
  st.on_press  = xr_logic.cfg_get_condlist(ini, section, "on_press", npc)

  st.tooltip  = ini:r_string_ex(section,"tooltip")
  if st.tooltip then
    npc:set_tip_text(st.tooltip)
  else
    npc:set_tip_text("")
  end

  st.anim = ini:r_string_ex(section,"anim")
  st.blending = ini:r_bool_ex(section,"anim_blend",true)
    if st.blending == nil then   
       st.blending = true 
    end
end

function create_fly_island(pos,lv,gv)
  local obj = create("fly_island",pos,lv,gv)
  netpacket:modify(obj, 
    "object_flags", -198,    -- 0xffffff3a object_flags
    "visual_flags", 1,      -- 0x1 visual_flags
    "skeleton_name", "idle",
    "skeleton_flags", 1,
    "physic_type", 3,      -- 0x3
    "mass", 100,
    "fixed_bones", "link")
  create("zone_fly_island",pos,lv,gv) -- —ç—Ç–æ –∞–Ω–æ–º–∞–ª–∏—è –Ω–∞–¥ –æ—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–≤–æ–≤–º, –¥—Ä—É–≥–æ–π –æ–±—ä–µ–∫—Ç
  return obj
end

–ù—É –∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω–æ–µ –æ—Ä—É–∂–∏–µ, –ø–∞—Ç—Ä–æ–Ω—ã –∫ –Ω–µ–º—É, –∫ –æ—Ä—É–∂–∏—é –≤ —Å–ª–æ—Ç–∞—Ö –æ–Ω –∏–≥–Ω–æ—Ä–∏—Ä—É–µ—Ç –Ω–∞ –æ–±–º–µ–Ω:
  npc:iterate_inventory(
    function (dummy,item)
      local a = true
      if npc:active_item() and item:id() == npc:active_item():id() then
        a = false
      end
      for i = 1,2 do
        if npc:item_in_slot(i) then
          if item:id() == npc:item_in_slot(i):id() then
            a = false
          end
          if system_ini():line_exist(npc:item_in_slot(i):section(), "ammo_class") then
            local tbl = mon_utils.parse_list(nil,npc:item_in_slot(i):section(),"ammo_class",true)
            if tbl and next(tbl) and tbl[item:section()] == true then
              a = false
            end
          end
        end
      end
      if system_ini():line_exist(item:section(), "quest_item") and system_ini():r_bool(item:section(),"quest_item") == true then
        a = false
      end
      if npc:active_item() then
        if system_ini():line_exist(npc:active_item():section(), "ammo_class") then
          local tbl = mon_utils.parse_list(nil,npc:active_item():section(),"ammo_class",true)
          if tbl and next(tbl) and tbl[item:section()] == true then
            a = false
          end
        end
      end
      if musor[item:section()] ~= nil then
        a = false
      end
      if a then
        table.insert(npc_items,item:id())
      end
    end
  ,nil)
üëç
